- **Jack**: "Alright, I’ve got 6 oak logs already. Jane, get ready to place the doors soon. John, let me know when you’ve got your wood. I’ll start crafting now! !craftRecipe("oak_planks", 24)"

The command `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 24)` indicates that Jack has converted his 6 oak logs into planks. Since 1 oak log produces 4 planks, 6 oak logs would produce:
\[ 6 \times 4 = 24 \text{ oak planks} \]

### Step 3: Crafting a Crafting Table
- **Jack**: "Alright, I've got 24 oak planks ready! I'll craft the crafting table now. !craftRecipe("crafting_table", 1)"

The command `!craftRecipe("crafting_table", 1)` indicates that Jack has crafted a crafting table. Crafting a crafting table consumes 4 oak planks, so after crafting the table, Jack still has:
\[ 24 - 4 = 20 \text{ oak planks remaining} \]

### Step 4: Placement of the Crafting Table
- **Jack**: "Alright, I've got 24 oak planks ready! I'll craft the crafting table now. !craftRecipe("crafting_table", 1)"
- **Jane**: "Got it, Jack! Let me know once the crafting table is placed, and I'll be ready to craft and place the doors!"

Although Jack mentions crafting the crafting table, there is no explicit mention of placing it yet. However, based on the context, we can assume he will place it soon.

### Step 5: Current Materials and Tools
- **Oak Planks**: Jack started with 24 oak planks but used 4 to craft the crafting table, leaving him with 20 oak planks.
- **Crafting Table**: Jack has crafted a crafting table but has not explicitly placed it yet.

### Final Answer
Given the information, Jack currently has:
- **20 oak planks** (after crafting the crafting table)
- **A crafting table** (crafted but not yet placed)

\[ \frac{28}{4} = 7 \text{ oak logs} \]

- **Crafting Table**: Jane has 1 crafting table.

     \[

   - Oak planks: 20

   - Jane is crafting the crafting table.
   - John is grabbing logs and starting to craft.

2. **Log Collection**:
   - John uses `!collectBlocks("oak_log", 3)` multiple times:
     - First: `!collectBlocks("oak_log", 3)`
     - Second: `!collectBlocks("oak_log", 3)`
     - Third: `!collectBlocks("oak_log", 3)`
   - Total logs collected by John: \(3 + 3 + 3 = 9\) oak logs.

3. **Plank Crafting**:
   - John crafts planks using `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 12)` and `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 20)`.
   - Each `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 4)` produces 16 planks, consuming 1 log.
   - Therefore:
     - `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 12)` produces \(12 \times 4 = 48\) planks.
     - `!craftRecipe("oak_planks", 20)` produces \(20 \times 4 = 80\) planks.
     - Total planks crafted: \(48 + 80 = 128\) planks.

4. **Door Crafting**:
   - John crafts doors using `!craftRecipe("oak_door", 2)` twice.
   - Each `!craftRecipe("oak_door", 1)` consumes 6 planks.
   - Therefore:
     - `!craftRecipe("oak_door", 2)` consumes \(2 \times 6 = 12\) planks per command.
     - Total planks consumed for doors: \(12 + 12 = 24\) planks.
